set filebase [format "%s%s" [format "%s%s" $basename "_"] $STAGE] 
top_pipeline_synth
# structural (synthesized) file as verilog                 
if {  $write_v == 1 } {
    set filename [format "%s%s" $filebase ".v"]
    write -format verilog -hierarchy -output $filename
}
